ChangeLog for Agar 1.3 (The Birth of an Era Obscured by Sulfur and Flames)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is a list of changes between the 1.2 and 1.3 release of Agar
(excluding the most trivial changes). For a list of the most notable
changes, see Release-1.3.txt.
